<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a> (29183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmaxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отма́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to signal with a flag</li>
<li>to finish waving</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmaxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отма́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover, to travel (a distance)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:километр.html>киломе́тров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>otmaxál</b> pjatʹ kilométrov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he traveled/covered five kilometers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wave away</li></ol>

***отмахиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмахиваться.html>отма́хиваться</a> (8911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отма́хивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmáxivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахиваться.html>отма́хиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmáxivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахнуться.html>отмахну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave/fan off/away</li>
<li>to wave away, to wave aside, to brush aside
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахиваться.html>отма́хиваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́са</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmáxivatʹsja</b> ot rešénija voprósa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn one's back on a problem; dismiss the matter with a wave of one's hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахиваться.html>отма́хиваться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam ot étovo tak ne <b>otmáxivatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't just brush it aside</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отма́хивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmáxivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмахнуться.html>отмахну́ться</a> (5777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отмахну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmaxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахнуться.html>отмахну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmaxnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахиваться.html>отма́хиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave/fan off/away</li>
<li>to wave away, to wave aside, to brush aside
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахнуться.html>отмахну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́са</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmaxnútʹsja</b> ot rešénija voprósa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn one's back on a problem; dismiss the matter with a wave of one's hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахнуться.html>отмахну́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam ot étovo tak ne <b>otmaxnútʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't just brush it aside</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отмахну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmaxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отмель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмель.html>о́тмель</a> (14650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмель.html>о́тмель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótmelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмель.html>о́тмели</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмель.html>о́тмели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмель.html>о́тмелей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sand <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a>, sand bank</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>мель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">melʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***отменить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отменить.html>отмени́ть</a> (4651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мени́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-menítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отменить.html>отмени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отменять.html>отменя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to abolish</li>
<li>to cancel, to countermand, to disaffirm, to reverse</li>
<li><i>law</i> to repeal, to rescind, to abrogate, to revoke, to call off</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отменять.html>отменя́ть</a> (14432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менять.html>меня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">menjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отменять.html>отменя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отменить.html>отмени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to abolish</li>
<li>to cancel, to countermand, to disaffirm, to reverse</li>
<li><i>law</i> to repeal, to rescind, to abrogate, to revoke, to call off</li></ol>

***отмерить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмерить.html>отме́рить</a> (17575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмерить.html>отме́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otméritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмерять.html>отмеря́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отме́ривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to measure, to measure off, to mete out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмерить.html>отме́рь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́жь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">semʹ raz <b>otmérʹ</b>, odín otréžʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look before you leap; better safe than sorry</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover (walk, drive, etc.) <i>a distance</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dole out, to give out (in small portions)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отметина.html>отме́тина</a> (25319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметина.html>отме́тина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmétina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметина.html>отме́тины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметина.html>отме́тины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметина.html>отме́тин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mark, sign</li>
<li>trace, imprint</li>
<li>different-colored spot on an animal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> distinctive trace of someone's influence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ме́тина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">métina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a> (1317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmétitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмечать.html>отмеча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mark</li>
<li>to note</li>
<li>to mark off, to make a note <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to mention, to point to, to record</li>
<li>to celebrate, to mark by celebration, to commemorate, to observe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">anniversary, ceremony</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to register <i>(out)</i>, to sign out</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметиться.html>отме́титься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmétitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмечаться.html>отмеча́ться</a></b>)

***отметка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тка</a> (7048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmétitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mark, to note</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mark, to label</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Vd. there for more
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mark, <a href = vnd.unilang:тик.html>tick</a></li>
<li>note, record
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорте</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmétka</b> v pásporte</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">record in the passport</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">academic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mark, grade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> како́му-л <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́ту</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmétka</b> po kakómu-l predmétu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">mark/grade in/for a subject</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поведение.html>поведе́нию</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmétka</b> po povedéniju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">mark/grade for conduct</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шие</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плохи́е</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тки</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xoróšije (ploxíje) <b>otmétki</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">high (low) marks/grades</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отметка.html>отме́тку</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyvodítʹ óbščuju <b>otmétku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">give an overall mark/grade</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mark, level

***отмечать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмечать.html>отмеча́ть</a> (3373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмечать.html>отмеча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmečátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отметить.html>отме́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mark</li>
<li>to note</li>
<li>to mark off, to make a note <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to mention, to point to, to record</li>
<li>to celebrate, to mark by celebration, to commemorate, to observe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">anniversary, ceremony</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to register <i>(out)</i>, to sign out</li></ol>

***отмечающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмечающийся.html>отмеча́ющийся</a> (4652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
